sarkaar ne anna hajaare paksh ke pramukh sadsy arvind kejariwal ke bhartiya rajasav seva (iares) chhodane ke kareeb chah saal baad antat: unka istipha manjuur kar liya
 Kejriwal paid nine lakh rupees to resolve the issue, after which his resignation has been accepted after 45 days
 unhone bataaya, ‘sarkaar ne iskar vibhaag se meraa istipha antat: sweekaar kar liya he
 i received the letter today
 ’ kejariwal ne farvari 2006 main iares se istipha de diya tha
 He was the Joint Commissioner of Income Tax at that time
 unhone pehle kaha tha ki vah bhugtan kiye gayi dhan ko waapas paane ke liye adaalat main ladenge

 pradhanmantri ko likhe patr main unhone kaha tha ki unke chah doston ko pareshaan nahin kiya jaae jinase unhone yah dhan udhaar liya he
 The 1995 batch IRS officer had decided to pay to respond to the frequent attacks of his opponents
 sarkaar kaa daawa he ki kejariwal ne puure vetan par adhyayan avkaash par jane ke baad teen saal kii anivaary seva puri karne se pehle pad chhodkar band ke niyamon kaa ulanghan kiya
 However, 43-year-old Kejriwal said that he had taken leave without pay and left the post fulfilling the terms of the bond
 kejariwal ne ek november, 2000 se do saal ke liye vaitanaik adhyayan avkaash liya tha
 He signed a bond stating that if he resigns or retires or does not work within three years of his study leave, he will have to return the salary
 kejariwal adhyayan avkaash ke baad ek november, 2002 ko seva par laute lekin 18 maheene baad unhone avaitnaik avkaash le liya
 The government argues that taking leave after 18 months is a violation of bond conditions but Kejriwal contended that he did not violate any provision and resigned from the post after a fixed period of three years after returning to work after study leave
 
 mukhya iskar ayukta ke karyaalay ne paanch agast ko kejariwal ko notice jari kar unase 9
 27 lakh rupees, which Kejriwal and other members of Team Anna termed as action taken by government officials on the instructions of their political masters
 kejariwal ne kaha tha ki vah pichley paanch saal se sarkaar ko samajhane kaa prayaas kar rahe hai ki unhone koi galat kaam nahin kiya he
 The Income Tax Department had set a deadline of October 27 for payment by Kejriwal but could not meet it
 unhone kaha tha ki is maamle main antim faisla karne se pehle unhen apane mitron se or adhik salaah mashvire kii jarurat he

 punjab ke up-mukhyamantri sukhbir singh badal ke laurence skool sanavar ko ek karod rupee daan ke rup main dene ke faisle kaa virodh hona shuru ho gaya he
 The opposition is raising the question that despite being a thriving school, why is such a huge amount being given to this school built in Himachal Pradesh? vipaksh ne badal par hamalaa karte hue kaha he ki sarkaar kii ye raashi rajya main vikaas kaary ke liye he

 vahiin duusari taraf sukhbir badal ne apana bachaav karte hue kaha he ki donneton kii is raashi ko cabinet ne manjuuri di he
 The opposition attacked Badal and said that this amount of the government is for the development work in the state
 ab vipaksh is mudde ko court main le jane kii dhamkee de rahaa he
 On the other hand, Sukhbir Badal has defended himself saying that this amount of donation has been approved by the cabinet
 himachal pradesh ke solan shahar main hamalaavaron ne ek head consteble ke bete kii goli markar hatya kar di jiske baad sthaneey logon ne virodh pradarshan shuru kar diya
 This information was given by the police today
 gaadi main savaar hamalaavaron ne motorcycle par ja rahe lakki par teen goliyaan chalaayin

 ) Expressing the UPA government's commitment to the right to privacy, Home Minister p Chidambaram said on Thursday that it would consider bringing technically competent National Technical Research Organization (NTRO) for telephone tapping under a ministry rather than the National Security Advisor So that it can be made accountable to the Parliament
 chidambaram ne kuch rajanetaaon ke telephonon kii kathith tanping ke parinamswaroop saarvajanik jivan main eemaandaaree ke mudde par padane vaale prabhaav tathaa is sambandh main sarkaar kii pratikriya par rajyasabha main hui alpakaalik charchaa ke jawaab main yah baat kahi
 He said that Prime Minister Manmohan Singh has instructed to get to the bottom of the telephone tapping case
 unhone kaha ki yadi jaanch main koi anadhikrut yaa gaiyrkanoonee telephone tanping kaa doshi paaya gaya to uske khilaaf karrwai kii jaaegi
 He said that if anyone is found guilty in this case, Parliament will be made aware of that
 antiaro kii charchaa karte hue chidambaram ne kaha ki yah abhi rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar ke adheen he or vah pradhanmantri ko soochna dete hai
 He said that it can be reviewed that NTRO be brought under any ministry so that it can be accountable to Parliament
 chidambaram ne kaha ki aatankwaadi, seemaa paar se aatank failaane vaale or sibar aparaadh karne vaale log atyaadhunik praudyogiki kaa istemaal karte hai
 He said that to tackle this, government agencies also need to be proficient in modern technology
 unhone kaha ki is baat kii jarurat he ki aise suraksha upaay banaae ja saken jisase nayi praudyogiki ke jariye logon kii niztaa kaa hanan nahin ho
 He categorically stated that the Home Secretary has not given permission to tap the phone of any politician
 lekin unhone is sambhaavna se bhi inkaar nahin kiya ki kisi netaa kii anadhikrut phone tanping kii gai ho
 Chidambaram said that phone tapping is ordered not only by the Union Home Secretary but also the Home Secretary of the states
 unhone kaha ki rajyon ko bhi is baat ke liye taiyaar kiya janaa chahie ki ve upyukt suraksha maanak apanaaen
 Denying allegations by some opposition leaders about the increasing role of lobbies in Indian democracy, the Home Minister said that lobbies or middlemen have no role in the government
 mantri banane kaa nirnay lobby nahin pradhanmantri karte hai
 Earlier, while participating in the discussion, the Leader of the Opposition said that the issue of phone tapping is an interference in privacy which is a gross violation of personal liberty in the Constitution
 unhone kaha ki yah behad gambhir maamla jo desh ke sansadeey loktantr se judaa hua he lihaaja is maamle kii jaanch ke liye sarkaar ko sansadeey samiti gathit kerani chahie
 Yoga teaches us the method of sitting, pranayama and meditation jointly
 niyamit rup se abhyaas karne vaale ko asankhya laabh praapt hote hai
 Yoga gives us many benefits such as benefits in health, mental strength, physical strength, protection of the body from wear and tear and purification of the body
 aaie jaanate hai 21 yogasana ke bare main or unhen karne ke tareeke ke bare main bhi
 1-ardha Chandrasana - While doing this asana, the body's position becomes half-lunar, hence it is called Ardha Chandrasana
 ardh kaa arth hota he aadha or chandrasana arthath chandra ke samaan kiya gaya asana
 This asana is performed by standing
 ardhachandrasana ko angreji main Half Moon Pose bhi kehete he
 This asana is a normal stretching and balancing pose that is especially beneficial for the lower back, abdomen and chest
 is asana ko karne se tanaav dur ho jaataa he
 Correct method of Ardha Chandrasana - To do this, first of all, stand with the heel-toes of both feet together
 donon haath qamar se sate hone chahie or apni gardan sidhi rakhen
 Then slowly keep both feet at a distance of one to one and a half feet from each other
 dhyaan rahe ki is asana kaa abhyaas karte vakt aapkaa merudand sidhaa rahe
 After this, raise the right hand and bring it parallel to the shoulder
 aapaki hatheli kaa rukh aasmaan kii ore hona chahie
 While doing this, keep in mind that your left hand remains on your waist
 ab bai ore jhuke, is dauraan aapkaa baayan haath swayan hi neeche khisakta jaayegaa
 Remember that the palm of the left hand should not be removed from the left leg
 isi sthiti main 30-40 second tak rahe, phir dhire dhire saamaanya sthiti main aaen
 If you are doing this for the first time, bend it as much as you can
 yahi prakriya duusari taraf bhi karen
 2-bhujang posture- First lie down on your stomach
 ab apane hatheliyon ko apane kandhe kii sidh main le kar aaen
 During this time, reduce the distance between your two feet and at the same time keep the feet straight and taut
 ab saans bharte hue body ke agle hisse ko naabhi tak uthaaen
 During this, keep in mind that there is not much stretch on your waist
 apni kshamta anusaar apni is avasthaa ko bana kar rakhen
 While practicing yoga, slowly breathe in and then release
 shuruaati mudra main waapas aate samay ek gahari saans ko chhodte hue vaapasi karen
 In this way a complete cycle of this posture ended
 ise aap apni kshamta anusaar doharaaen
 3-bal asana-bal means - baby or child, in Balasana we bow our arms and body forward like an infant with a thunderbolt
 yah asana behad aasaan zarur he magar kaaphi laabhadaayak bhi he
 Relaxes the muscles of the waist and this asana also removes constipation
 man ko shant karne vaala ye asana tantrika tantra ko shant karata he
 Procedure for performing Balasana (shishuasana) - Sit on your ankles, place the hips on the heel, bend forward and apply the forehead on the ground
 haathon ko sharir ke donon ore se aage kii ore badhaate hue jameen par rakhen, hatheli akaash kii ore (agar ye aaramdaayak naa ho to aap ek hatheli ke upar duusari hatheli ko rakhkar maathe ko aaraam se rakhen
 )
 dhire se chaati se jaangho par dabaav den
 Keep the status quo
 dhire se uthakar edi par baith jaaen or ridh kii haddi ko dhire dhire sidhaa karen
 veg out
 4-marger asana-apane ghutanon or haathon ke bal aaen or sharir ko ek mej kai tarah bana len
 Make the upper part of the table with your back and make the legs around the table with hands and feet
 apane haath kandhon ke thik neeche, hatheliyaan jameen se chipki hui rakhen or ghutanon main putthon jitna antar rakhen
 Keep the neck straight in front of you
 saans lete hue apni thodi ko upar kii ore sar ko peeche kii ore le jaaen, apni naabhi ko jameen kii ore dabaaen or apni qamar ke niche ke hisse ko chat kii ore le jaaen
 Shrink both folds
 is sthiti ko banaaen rakhen ore lambii gahari saansen lete or chhodte rahen
 Now we will do the opposite
 saans chhodte hue thodi ko chaati se lagaaein ore peeth ko dhanush aakaar main jitna upar ho sake utana uthaaen, putthon ko dhilaa chhod den
 Keep this position for some time and then come to the position as before
 is prakriya ko paanch se 6 baar doharaaen or vishram karen
 5-nataraja Asana - This asana is named after Lord Shiva
 shuruyaat main ise karne main thodaa kathinaayee aa sakati he parantu iske niyamit abhyaas se ise aasaani se kiya ja saktaa he
 First of all, stand in a relaxed posture
 sharir kaa bhaar baayen pair par sthapit karen or daaen ghutane ko dhire dhire moden or pair ko jameen se upar uthaaen
 Bend your right leg and follow it
 daaen haath se daaen takhne ko pakaden
 Raise the left arm to shoulder height
 saans chhodte hue baayen pair ko zamin par dabaaen or aage kii ore jhuken
 Move the right leg away from the body
 sir or gardan ko merudand kii sidh main rakhen
 Stay in this posture for 15 to 30 seconds
 isse aapkaa body banlence bahut acha hoga or aapkaa sharir adhik se adhik lacheela banegaa
 This posture will improve blood circulation in the hands and feet, improve the nervous system
 6-gomukh asana-gomukh asana sharir ko sudaul or sudrudh banane vaala yoga he
 This yoga pose is done by sitting
 is mudra main mul rup se daanon haath, qamar or merudand kaa vyaayaam hota he
 Gomukh Asana is a very beneficial exercise for women
 palathi lagaakar baithen
 Bend your left leg and bring the left sole behind the right hips
 daaen pair ko modakar daaen talave ko baayen hips ke peeche laaen
 Place your palms on the feet
 hips ko neeche kii ore halkaa dabaaen or sharir ke upree bhaag ko sidhaa rakhen evam sir ko sidhaa or sathulit karen
 Move the hands backwards by bending the left elbow
 saans khinchate hue daaen haath ko upar uthaaen
 Move the right hand backward by bending the right elbow
 donon haathon kii ungaliyon ko aapas main joden
 Lightly pull both hands in your direction
 7-halasana-halasana halasana main sharir ko hal kii mudra main rakhaa jaataa he
 It is very important for the body to be flexible for this asana
 farsh par peeth ke bal sidhe let jaaen or apane donon haathon ko bhi bilkul aaraam kii mudra main jameen par sidhe rakhen
 Taking long breath, raise your legs above the floor with the help of abdominal muscles and keep both feet standing at a 90 degree angle
 saamaanya rup se lagaataar saans lete hue apane kulhon or peeth ko haath kii sahaayta se farsh se upar uthaaen
 Now, while moving your feet above the head, bend at a 180 degree angle until your toes touch the floor
 aapaki peeth farsh par lambavat honi chahie
 Initially you will have difficulty in being in this posture but after a little effort you can do it easily
 is prakriya ko dhire-dhire or aaraam se karen
 But also keep in mind that you do not have to put pressure on your neck nor push it towards the ground
 ab saamaanya avasthaa main aa jaaen or sharir ko thodi der aaraam den
 Keep breathing and feel relaxed
 8-sethu baandh asana-sethu baandh yoga mudra se merudand lacheela hota he saath hi gardan se tanaav bhi dur hota he
 Lie on your back
 ghutanon ko modakar talvon ko acchhee tarah se zamin par tikaaen
 Place the arms on both sides of the body with the ground
 is avasthaa main hatheliyaan jameen par tiki honi chahie
 While exhaling, pull the bones of the spine and press the waist gently towards the ground
 gahari saans lete hue pairon ko jameen kii ore dabaaen evam pedu ko jitna ho sake upar kii ore uthaaen
 Remain in this posture for 30 seconds to 1 minute
 saans chhodte hue dhire dhire saamaanya avasthaa main laut aaen
 9- Rocking Chair Yoga - Performing rocking chair yoga transmits energy to the bones of the spine
 saath hi sharir main rakt kaa sanchaar tej gati hota he
 10-sukhasana-sukhasana holds both legs pressed in a cross posture, also known as the lotus posture
 dhyaan ke liye yah upyukt asana hota he
 Lay the palathi by sitting easy on flat ground
 apane sir gardan or peeth ko sidhaa rakhen, unhen jhukaaen nahin
 Leave the shoulders slightly loose
 donon haathon ko ghutanon par tathaa hatheliyon ko upar kii or rakhen
 Raise your head slightly and close your eyes
 ab apana dhyaan apni shwasan kriya par lagaaein or lambi or gahari saans lete rahen
 You can do this asana for 5-10 minutes at any time by sitting in solitude
 agar aap aadhyatmik drushti se yah yoga kar rahe hai to purv yaa uttar disha main ise karen
 11
 namaskara asana-namaskara asana kisi bhi asana kii shuruyaat main kiya jaataa he
 It is quite simple
 12-tarasana-sabase pehle sidhe khadey ho jaaen
 Then keep both your legs together and keep both hands straight at the waist
 is vakt aapkaa sharir sthir rahanaa chahie
 That is, the body weight should be the same on both your legs
 ab dhire-dhire haathon ko kandhon ke samaanaantar laaen
 Now join the fingers of both the palms and take them above the head
 ab saans bharte hue apane haathon ko upar kii ore khinchie, jab tak aapako kandhon or chaati main khinchaav mahasoos nahin hone lage
 At the same time raise the heel of the feet also and cautiously stand on the feet
 ab finger lock lagaakar haathon ke panjon ko upar kii ore mode den
 At this time your neck should be straight and the palms should be towards the sky
 dhyaan rakhen ki aapaki pairon kii anguliyon par sharir kaa santulan bana rahe
 After stopping for a while in this position, while exhaling, bring the hands back over the head
 dhire dhire ediyon ko bhi bhoomi par tikaa den or donon haathon ko bhi neeche laate hue qamar se sataakar pehle vaali sthiti yane kii vishram mudra main aa jaaen
 Do this asana regularly at least 10 times
 13-trikon mudra-trikon asana kaa abhyaas khadaa rahakar kiya jaataa he
 This asana resembles lateral angulation
 is yoga se hips, pair, takhnon, pairon or chaati kaa vyaayaam hota he
 It is also beneficial for Mudra Qamar
 is mudra kaa abhyaas kis prakaar karnaa chahie
 What is the state of this currency and what is the benefit of it? Let's see it
 vishram kii mudra main khadey ho jaaen
 Spread the right leg 3 to 5 feet
 baayen pair ko 45 degree or daaen pair ko 90 degree mode
 Breathing, spread the arms at the height of the shoulders
 is sthiti main hatheliyon ko zamin kii disha main rakhana chahie
 Move the hips backward and bring the upper part of the body to the right
 saans chhodte hue daayi hatheli ko daane pair ke peeche le jaaen
 Move the left hand up towards the ceiling
 sir ko baayen haath kii disha main ghumaakar dekhen
 In this condition, the spinal cord should be straight and neck relaxed
 is mudra main 10 se 30 second tak bane rahen
 14-konasana-konasana is as easy to do, equally beneficial for the body
 pairon ke bich main 2 fit kaa antar rakhen
 Balance equal weight on both legs
 shwaas lete hue donon haathon ko failaate hue sir ke upar le jaaen or hatheliyon ko joden
 Place the hands in a dome-like position by connecting the fingers together
 dhyaan rahe ki haath kaan se choote hue jaaen
 Breathing out, bend to the right
 yah dhyaan den ki haath kohniyon se mude nahin
 Keep pressure on the ground with your feet
 shroni bahine or rahen
 Stay in this position
 sharir main jhukate hue khinchaav banaae rahen
 In this position, inhale deeply and release
 shwaas lete hue punah saamaanya sthiti main khadey hon
 Exhale, bring both hands down
 baayen ore yahi prakriya doharaaen
 15-utsasana- "ustra" is a Sanskrit language and it means camel
 ustrasana ko angreji main “camel Pose” kaha jaataa he
 Ustrasana is an intermediate back-bending yoga posture that opens the Anahata (heart cycle)
 is asana se sharir main lacheelaapan aata he, sharir ko takat milti he tathaa pachan shakti bad jaati he
 Sit on the mat with your knees and place both hands on the ax
 ghutane kandho ke samanaantar ho tathaa pairon ke talave akaash kii taraf ho
 Breathing, pull the spinal cord towards the anterior limb as if being pulled from the navel
 gardan par bina dabaav daalen tatasth baithe rahen
 Keep taking some breath in this situation
 saans chhodte hue apane praarambhik sthiti main aa jaaen
 Bring the hands back to your waist and be straight
 16-vajrasana-is asana ke abhyaas se sharir majboot banataa he
 It is a meditative posture
 yah ek maatr aisa asana he jise khaane ke baad bhi kar sakate he
 You can do this asana both day or evening
 vajrasana karne ke liye kisi saafe samtal jagah par dari bichhaaen
 Then sit on your knees and spread the toes behind, and put one toe on the other thumb
 is mudra main aapke ghutane paas-paas kintu ediyaan alag-alag honi chahie
 Your hip should be in the middle of both the paws and the heels are towards the hips
 ab apni hatheliyon ko ghutano par rakhen
 Practice Vajrasana according to your ability
 baad main waapas saamaanya avasthaa main aa jaaen
 To perform Vajrasana, take the first 5 minutes after meals, then do it
 17-vrikshasana-vrikshasana kaa arth he vriksh ke samaan mudra
 This asana is performed by standing
 nataraj asana ke samaan yah asana bhi shaareerik santulan ke liye bahut hi laabhprad haivrikshasana karne ke liye sidhaa tanakar khadey ho jaaie
 Put the weight of the body on the left leg and bend the right leg
 daaen pair ke talave ko ghutanon ke upar le jaakar baayen pair se lagaaie
 Bring both palms near the chest in prayer posture
 apane daaen pair ke talave se baayen pair ko dabaaie
 Press the soles of the left foot towards the ground
 saans lete hue apane haathon ko sir ke upar le jaaie
 Keep the head straight and look at the front
 is mudra main 15 se 30 second tak bane rahiye
 Repeat this pose 2 to 5 times on both sides
 18-dandasana-dandasana karne ke liye sabase pehle kisi saaf-svachh sthaan par kambal aadi bicha len
 Now sit upright and keep both feet parallel to the face and keep it straight
 sir ko bilkul sidhaa rakhen
 Fold your toes inward and push the soles outward
 19-adhomukhi shwaan asana-adhomukh swaan asana ek kute (shwaan / swaan) kii tarah saamne kii ore jhukne kaa pratikatmak he isliye ise adhomukh swaan asana kehete hai
 Come on your hands and feet
 sharir ko ek mez kii sthiti main le aaen
 Your back should be like the top of the table and both arms and legs are like the legs of the table
 saans chhodte hue qamar ko upar uthaaen
 Make your knees and elbows straight while strengthening) Make an inverted v shape from your body
 haath kandho ke jitne duuri par hon
 Legs equal to waist distance and parallel to each other
 pair kii unglia bilkul saamne kii taraf hon
 Press your palms to the ground, strengthen it with the help of shoulders
 gale ko tana hua rakhte hue kaanon ko bahon se sparsh karaaen
 Take long deep breaths, remain in a state of downward swan
 apni nazaren naabhi par banaae rakhen
 While exhaling, bend the knee and return to the table position
 vishram karen
 20-shavasana - You have to feel relaxed while doing it
 ab apni peeth ke sahare let jaaen or dhyaan rakhe kii is avasthaa main aapke pair zamin par bilkul sidhe hone chahie
 Keep both your hands at least 5 inches away from the body
 haathon ko is tarah rakhe ki donon haath kii hatheliyaan aasmaan kii disha main ho
 Now you have to leave every body part loose, and also close the eyes
 halki-halki saanse len
 At this time your complete focus should be on breaths
 man main duusare kisi bhi vichaar ko aane naa den
 While doing this easy, if you feel any kind of problem in the waist or spine, then you can put a blanket or pillow below the knee
 21-utkar asana-donon pairon ko milakar rakhie or sidhe khadey rahen
 Keep the feet and fingers together
 donon ghutanon ko modate hue neeche baithiye or ediyon ko uthaa lijie taaki puure sharir kaa santulan donon pairon kii ungaliyon par rahe
 Keep both knees together
 ridh ko sidhaa rakhane kaa prayaas karen
 Keep both hands adjacent to the ground to facilitate balance
 iske baad donon kohniyon ko janghaon par rakhie or haathon kii ungaliyon ko aapas main milakar thudi ke neeche rakhie
 Be aware of the breath and try to maintain balance
 ek-do minute tak is sthiti main ruken or saamne kisi ek bindu par ekagra karen

 ‘‘pehla paridrishy vibhaajan ke baad nayaa shashan khadaa karne ke liye pakistan ke raajnneetik or sanvaidhanik sangharsh kaa he

 jiske falswaroop baad main charampanthi takatein majboot huin
 '' Comments ‘‘doosraa paridrishy varsh 1979 ke baad yani irani kranti ke baad kii sthiti main soviet sangh dwaara afghanistan par kiye gaye hamale or pakistan dwaara puure pashchimi jagat, china evam saudi arab ke netritv main puure muslim samudaay kii madad se iskaa virodh karne main nibhaai gai bhoomika ke baad kaa he
 This strengthened the extremists and the terrorists
 ’’ He wrote, "the equations between Pakistan and India helped strengthen the reactionary elements at the expense of liberal elements within Pakistan
" chauthaa kaarak jarb-e-ajb oparation ke baad pakistan kii sthiti ko mana jaataa he
 This operation was carried out by the Pakistani army to take refuge in the federally administered tribal areas and to eradicate the terrorists who have prepared the entire infrastructure for their activities
 ’’ Regarding indo-pak relations, he said, "pakistan-india relationship has an impact on extremist elements among Muslims in Pakistan
" iske alaava kashmir ghati kii tanaavpurn sthiti bhi ek pralobhan kaa kaam karti he or charampanthi tatwon ko ‘apane saathi muslimon ko mukt karaane ke liye jihad karne’ ko protsaahit karti he
 "they believe that normalizing relations between the two countries will help the pluralistic and liberal forces of Pakistan and at the same time improve the condition of minorities in both countries
" kasuri kaa yah bhi maananaa he ki mujahidin kii gatividhiyon ke prati shuruaati samarthan ke baavjood pashchim or khaastaur par pakistan ko is jihad ke liye baari keemat chukaani pad rahi he or ye ab bhi iske palatwaar kaa shikaar ban rahe hai
 In a recent issue of Equator Line magazine, he wrote, "over time the West and Pakistan had to deal with the growing relationship between terrorist groups with different opinions
 pakistan ko yah bhi pataa chalaa ki kashmir main lard rahe kuch samooh uske apane nagarikon or suraksha balon par bhi aasaani se hamale bol sakate hai
 '' is patrika main unhone likhaa, ‘‘kai maamalon main khufia agency or kanoon pravartan agenciyon ko bhi nishaanaa banaaya gaya
 Public opinion in Pakistan is now turning against the activities of violent groups, irrespective of any reason for this violence
 ’’ patrika ke liye lekh likhane waalon main sabhi pakistani mul ke log hai
 Kasuri said that it is now widely accepted in the middle class people and large sections of the media that Kashmir and other issues with India cannot be resolved through violence of non-governmental elements and although these activities have led to international level But it has caught the attention of the people but after the 9 / 11 attacks, it became clear that the international community is losing patience towards such activities
 kasuri ne likhaa, ‘‘yah ahsaas ho gaya he ki pakistan or bharat ko kashmir or anya muddon ko sulajhane ke liye baatcheet ke jariye samaadhaan nikaalnaa hoga
 i do not want to give the message that at the time when i took office, the feeling of cooperation towards jihadi groups in all sections was over
 lekin kashmir ke mudde ke prati pakistan kii drudh patibaddhta ke kaaran kuch virgon main jihadiyon kii gatividhiyon ke prati sahanubhuti kaa tatv bahut kam lekin ,hameshaa rahegaa
 '' kasuri ke anusaar, pakistan main kattarpanth ke udai ke kai kaaran hai or is mudde ko kam se kam chaar paridrishyon main dekhnaa madadgaar ho saktaa he
 "the first scenario is about the political and constitutional struggle of Pakistan to create a new regime after partition
" isane ulema kii bhoomika ko pakkaa karte hue general jiya-ul-haq ke tahat iskaa vistaar hone diya
 As a result, the extremist forces later strengthened

 Malinga also did not deny the news of retiring from cricket after the World T20 during the Asia Cup
